2b3(11): sa bsam me khya// re yang sangs rgyas dgongs pa yin// sbru las ma byung rkyen med pas// dngos por ma yin rtag chad med// de yang sangs rgyas dgongs pa yin// spyod dang bral bas sgo srung med// mtha' dbus med par rgyu 'bras cig/ de yang sangs rgyas dgos
2b4(11): papayin/ de yang sems dpa' rdo rje nyon// gcig las thams cad rdzogs pa ste// sangs rgyas rnams kyi dgongs pa de// tshig tu mtshon nas slad ci bcos// thams cad rang byung ye shes nyid// rdzogs pa chen po lta ba thams cad kyi snying po'i rgyud las/
2b5(11): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dgongs pa 'astan pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// / de nas 'dus pa'i tshogs rnams la// kun rig sems kyi rgyal po yis// chos rnams gtan la das pa'i phyir// don gyi snying po 'di rtogs pa'i tha /
2b6(11): ba bzhi ru mdor bsdus nas// 'phrang chen drug gri gtan la dbab// man ngag lnga yis kha bzlas la// gtan tshigs bzhi yis yid ches bya// de yang sems dpa' rdo rje khyod// rtsa ba bzhi ru mdor bsdus nas// gzhi nges lta ba phyogs med dang // don dang mi 'bral
2b7(11): ting 'dzin pas// spang blang med pa'i spyod pa dang // re ba med pa'i 'bras bu la/ rnam pa bzhi ru sdus pa yin// 'khor ba'i snying po da nyon cig/ gtan la dbab pa'i phreng drug ni// lta ba skye med don gyi 'phrang // brtsal ba med pas lhun gyis grub// rang blo 'gyur med
3a1(11): ting 'dzid 'brang / sgom pa rad pang ye shes gas pa// nyams kyi rin pa gdams ngag 'phrang// po rings ma 'khrugs dbyis su slebs/ lba ba shes dab blo'i 'brang // chas rnams kyi khyad par 'byed// swa ba sreng med ga la sa'i/
3a2(11): 'brang / ji tsam bskams kyang don med 'byam// phyir rgol rtsod chang tshig gis 'brang // gzhan tshig skyon la rang gzhung bskya// de dag drug gis gtan dang ba// de yang sems dpa' rdo rje nyon// mnangag lnga la la bzlas pa/ sangs rgyas sems can rgyu ga cis
3a3(11): phyir/ gnyis su med par la bzla'o// 'khor 'das rtsa kha cig pa'i phyir/ lhun gyis grub par la bzla'o// gtsang dang mi 'atsang gzhi gcig pas/ blang dor med/ pang la bzla'o// skyon dang yon tan dbyer med pas// bsgom du med par la bzla'o// 'khrul dang ma rig
3a4(11): dngos med pas/ dug lnga ye shes lnga ru lA 'dra'o// de yang 'dus pa'i tshogs rnams kun// yid ches pa yi gtan tshigs ni// rang bzhin skye med gtan tshig kyi// lhun gyis grub par yid ches bya// rol pa 'gag med gtan tshig kyi// gang yang mi 'gal yid
3a5(11): chen bya/ mtshan nyid gnyis med gtan tshigs kyis// chos rnams gcig par yid ches bya// ngob blo gros gtan tshigs kyis// col ba med par yi ches bya// snying po'i don 'di rtogs 'dod pas// dam pa'i rgyud don gnas par gyis// rdzogs pa chen
3a6(11): po lta ba thams cad kyi snying po las// chos rnam kyi rang bzhin gtan la dbab pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// / de nas kun rigs rgyal po yis// 'dus pa'i tshog la bka' stsal pa// don dam snang bcung rim pa ni// gas sngags rnam
3a7(11): zici ba yin dang rnams ri nga rdzogs byanas// rma sasam gyu lams rgyas nas// dam pa'i mon gyiganye ldan zhing/ srid gzhus kyi nga med pa'i tham la su dpan de// dbang nags kyis dag bzhin// cig thus nas kyi do ldan
3b1(11): skal ldan ma'i mtshan nyid ni// bla ma la gus dang bar ldan// ser sna chung la brtson 'grub che// don gsang thub la shes rab zab// tshul shes dang bzang rnams kyi gter // de dang mi ldan 'di bstan nA// sangs rgyas kun gyi bka' 'acag ste// mtshams med/
3b2(11): sdig pa'i char mi 'od// dmyal ba'i 'og gzhi byed pang gsungs// rdzogs pa chen po rgya la thams cad kyi snying po las// snod bcung bstan pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// / de nas kun rig rgyal po yi// sems dpa' rdo rjes don lus pa/
3b3(11): 'gro drug sdug bsngal ci las byung // mu steg rtag char ji ltar 'phrul// theg pa'i rim pa gang ltar 'byung // de skad gsol pa'i tshig gsan nas/ kun rig rgyal pos bka' stsal pa// rtsa ba gcig pa'i sems nyid la// 'gro drug sdug bsngal 'byub ba
3b4(11): ni rdzag pa sbrul du la ni ma bzhin// ma rig lhan cig rgyu nyid las/ kun rtags mi dag rkyen rgyas / ma sum las spyan bya'i phyor// bas chags lngal longs spyod nas// dmyal ba dang skyes ma rdzogs mtha'// yi dgas mi gtsang mthong yul snu
3b5(11): mi yis mthong yul bzhin du snang // byol long ngam 'grog gyen thung snang // lha ma yin gyi go mtshon mthong // lha rnams rin chen sna bdun mthong // de dag 'gro drug sdug bsngal yin// rdzogs pa chen po lta ba thams cad kyi snying pa las/ @
3b6(11): drug gi sdug bsngal bstan pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// de nas 'dus tshogs rnams la/ kun rigs sems kyi rgyal po yis// mu steg 'a khral lugs bka' stsal pa/ yongs mtha' 'dzin pa'i lta ba ni// 'gyur ba bzhi
3b7(11): dgam pardza/ mams cad 'dag ni byis papadas/ rgyu thas lag pa'i 'tshul thums kyis/ rang 'am mo zer 'khor ba srug/ ma dang bye ma 'di ba 'ang// yin ca par 'ad 'ani/ sra mos smras pa'i chos rnams thab/ rdus thams
4a1(11): las 'byung ba'i phyir/ 'byung ba lnga bzhi pang thim nas/ mi shi thal ba drung khyer 'dra// de yang sems dpa' rdo lnga khyod// gnyis ga'i gzhi mdor mu stegs ni// rig bye gsang bang spru la ste// gzhi ni ngas med pa la/ swa/
4a2(11): pagang yang mi 'anog 'ad// gdon gyi zin pa'i nad pa bzhin// sems kyi rang bzhin ma gos na// 'byung chen btos kyi rnamakha' bzhin// thug rje'i phreng zhag thag cha nas// dmyal ba'i 'bras chung the tshom med// rdzogs pa rgyan po lta ba thams cad kyi snying /
4a3(11): las/ mu stegs 'khrul tshul bstan pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// // de nas 'dus pa'i cho ga rnams la// kun rig rgyal pos bka' stsal pa/ sems nyid rnga ba nyid kyi sku// mthun dpe me long lta gu la// gzugs brnyan theg pa rim dgu byung // de yang gang
4a4(11): dang gang zhe na/ 'phags pa nyan thos lta ba ni/ mdo sde bye bla rnam gnyis chos// cho ga yul gyi khyad pa las// lus gdungs sems kyi brtson bzu kyang // rdul dang shes pa gnyis 'dod pas// glang chen 'dam du bying ba bzhin// lus ngag las kyi rtso
4a5(11): yin/ 'bras bu med pa snying rje gnas// bla ma dag la mi rten par// rang sems don la lo sbyang phyir// rten 'brel phyin pa gtsang bcad nas// rang bzhin med papa bde 'cha' ba// brtsan par mi 'gyur nyams pa'i phyir// nor bu rgyal srid sgom pa 'dra// chos rnams seMs
4a6(11): gyirang bzhin la// kun rdzob dang ni 'on dam du// so sor rtog pa'i ye shes rab kyis// bden pa gnyis su rnam par phye// cig gshigs nas ni cig tshol ba// chu bdag zla ba nges 'dzin 'dra// de yang sems dpa' rdo rje khyod// thams cad rtsa bcig ma yin// rang gi sa
4a7(11): kyi snying pa 'don bsam gyi mi khyab ye shes 'bar // bsam med pa dug 'dzin pa// byis pa de ni thun pa ste// mun pa'i skye mched nyid du 'gyur/ rdzogs pa chen po lta 'a thams cad kyi snying po las// rgyu mtshan nyid kyi lta ba bstan pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o//
4b1(11): nas kun rig rgyal po yis// 'dus pa'i tshogs la bka' stsal pa// chos nyid sdung pa'i ngang las ni// dag pa bzhi'i sgong zhug nas// yo byad phyi la gtsong 'dzin cing // kun rdzob lha'i dkyil 'khor ru// rgyu nyid pa'i ting 'dzin gyis// sku'i gzugs brnyan phyag 'tshan
4b2(11): dang / bzlas brjod gtsa sgra dus tshigs kyis// rgyu rkyen tshogs pa'i nus mthu yis// rigs gsung dkyil 'khor lhar gsal yang // dngos grub gzhan nas re ba yis// khyinan 'dab chag snyeg pa 'dra// rab sems dbye ba med pa la// u pa ya yi lta ba ni// gong 'og lta spyod
4b3(11): gnyis 'dzin pa// ne tse mi skad bzlos pa 'dra// yo ga rnal 'byor sems dpa' yis// phyag rgya bzhi'i sgor zhugs nas// yo byad gtso ru mi 'dzin pa'i// don dam skye 'gag med pa yis// lha'i dkyib 'khor 'phags pa'i sku// rnam par snang mdzad chen po yi// chos
4b4(11): dbyings dag gi byin rlabs pas// lha dang bdag tu mnyam pa yis// dam tshig ye shes lhang gsal kyang // rgyal srid med pa'i blon po 'dra// de yang 'dus pa'i tshogs rnams kun// bla ma'i don med nam rtags kyis// dmigs pa can la sems gtad kyang // rnam par grol
4b5(11): ra mi 'gyur te/ na mkha' dag la 'jin pa 'dra// rdzogs pa chen po lta ba thams cad kyi snying po la/ phyi 'a thub pa rgyudan kyi lta ba bstan pa'i le'u ste brgyad pa'o// // de nas 'dus pa'i tshog chen la/ kun rig rgyal pos bka' stsal// 'khor ba mya ngan 'das 'das
4b6(11): pa'i sa/ sems gi rtag ci skyes kyang // mtshan ma dngas po ma grub pas// dpe na rnam kha'i ser bubazhin// yod ma dbus las mi gnas pas// sku gsum ye shes lhun gyis grug/ yul sems dbye ba med pa la// thabs dang shes rab spang zhugs nas/
4b7(11): ti 'dzin gsung gyis lhur bsgoms pas// grib ma gzugasu gyur pa 'dra// phyi na chos rnams ma lus kun// yid dang kun gzhi gnyis 'dus nas/ kun gzhi rnam dag mkha' klong du// rnam rtogs mtsham mtshan ma gang spyod kyang // namakha'i gza' skad brtsal med
5a1(11): bzhin// kun bzang de chen thabs kyi gtso// kun tu tha ma dadi can mkha'// 'du 'bral med pa'i chos su ni// sechen gnyis rig pa'i rgyal// nges pa'i gsal blo ma shes par// kun parab spyad pas don mi rtags/ nyi ma smin gyis smin pa /
5a2(11): sems nyid rtsol ba med pa la/ bsam pa'i dbang gis bsgrur byas pas// 'khor ba'i rgya mtshodar yengs gyur te// mi shes pa la de ltar snang // rdzogs pa chen po lta ba thams cad kyi snying po las// bskyed rdzogs gnyis bstan pa'i le'u ste dgu pa'o//
5a3(11): de nas sems dpa' rdo rje yis// 'dus pa'i tsho ga la phan gdags phyir// kun rig sems kyi rgyal po la// yid kyi dran pas 'di skad gsol// chos rnams semasu 'dus pa yi// spyan gyis grub pa'i lha gang // mtshan ma zil gyis ji ltar gtsang // 'gro drug g.yang
5a4(11): sa ji ltar gtsang / ye shes don la ji ltar bsgom// mnyam pa'i rgyal pos bshad du gsol// de skad zhus pa'i tshigs gsan nas// kun rig sems kyi rgyal pos yis 'dus pa'i 'khor la bka' stsal pa// sems su chos rnams gcig pa ni// 'khor ba mya ngan 'ang
5a5(11): pa'i chos/ sgyu ma rnam gnyis spyod yul te// log rtogs ye shes tha dad kyang // sems kyi chos nyid nga du gcig/ de yis de nyid mtshon pa'i dpe// na mkha' 'ja' tshon ji bzhin du// yul gyis tha snyad mtshan ma rnams// rang gi sems kyi brtags pa'i
5a6(11): phyir/ phyi nang chos rnams ma lus pa// rig rgyud med phyir semasu gcig/ de nyid lhun gyis grub pa ni// 'gro la sems nyid gnyis med de// ji ltar dmigs shing bsam par snang // dper na yid bzhin nor bu bzhin// de ni lhun gyis grub pa'i gzhi// de yang
5a7(11): sems dpa' rdo rje khyod// kun la khyab pa'i rig pa yin// 'dus ma byas pa'i doni rtogs pas// ye shes rig pa gcig yin no// de yang gang dang gang zhe na// kun gyi mnyam nyid rgyal ba'i thugs// ma lus sems can thams cad la// chos sku khyab pa brdal gi/
5a8(11): 'byung ba lnga la rag ma lus// mi 'gyur lo ma byed rdo rje 'dra/ bla mas don bstan rnal 'byor pas// the tshom med par sems nyid rtog// thabs su cig la ma 'dres pa// ka shi ras kyi rin chen 'dra// de yang sems dpa' rdo rje khyod// sems kyi snying po'i don
5a9(11): rtogs nas/ sems su snang ba'i mtshan ma rnams// rang byung ye shes yang dag shar// spros med ngo bo lhun gyis gya // srid pa gsung ni rang gis rkyen// ma bcos pa'i ye shes yin// brtsal du med pa'i sems nyid la// rgyu 'bras gnyis ka
5a10(11): mya ngan 'das/ khams gsum/ spros med dbyings su gcig/ yul du snang ba thams cad kyang / ya nas dbyer med mnyam par gnas// thams cad rang byung 'gag pa med/ gdod nas ma skyes lhun gyis grub// thams cad ye nas dbyer med par// dbyings
5a11(11): nyid na mkha' lta bu'i ngang // de'i ngang du thams cad 'dus// rgyu dang rkyen la ma ltos shing // dus gsum dbyer med mnyam lta ba/ dper na na mkha'i nyi ma bzhin// ma rig mun pa thams cad 'joms// de nyid rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// lta ba yin pa'i don nyid
5a12(11): la/ ma nor rig pa gcig yin te/ lhun grub 'bras bu cig pu stan/ rdzog pa chen po'i lta ba thams cad kyi snying po las// lhun gyi grub pa bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu pa'o// / de nas sems dpal rdo rje la// kun rig sems kyi rgyal po yis
5a13(11): mtshan mthil gyis mnan pa'i phyir// ma rig mun pa lta bu la// rig pa'i ye shes bstan pa'i thabs// rig pa'i ye shes dbang byed bka' stsal pa// de'i dbang po dpa' bstan te// bram ze gtsang ma khrus gsol te// rgyal srid dag la khrus gsol te// rgyal srid
6a1(11): ngag la dbang sgyur zhing // don gyi snod la rang byung 'chang // de don shes rabaM drang thams cad kyis// 'dus ma byas pa dpe nyid la// rang gi tshad dang ldan pa la// sems ni drag tu gtad par bya// dbedan gyi gling rta 'dul bzhin// rang gi shes
6a2(11): pa ma yengs pa/ dra gzhan par na rtsol ba gnon// tshad zin don la gnas par bya// de yang khams dang sbyar byas la// khams bde thun thung du bya// yangs na lags la cung zad bcag/ rtag ni lus sems gnyis 'byung ste// lus tri dang ShA chi ma 'byung // sems
6a3(11): ni bde la btang dka' ste// rang sems rtsal gyis rtags rnams 'byung // rtog pa med par gnas pa ni// bya ba btang ba'i skyes bu bzhin// ci la mi gnas rang bzhin la// ma yengs gsal ba lhug par bzhag/ gdod nas na mkha'i sprin bzhin du// byung yang gzhi
6a4(11): la gnod med ltar// sems kyi rtsol ba chad zin na// rtogs med mi sgrib bcos mi dgos// de yis ye shes ngos zin na// thog ma med par bsags pa yi// rnam rtog sprin spu dpag med pa// stong nyid skad cig rig pa yis// rnam rtog stong pa'i bang du sangs
6a5(11): sangs rgyas sems can la sogs pas// kun kyang rang byung ye shes nyid// stong nyid skad cig rig pa yis/ rnam rtog stong pa'i ngang du sangs// sangs rgyas sems can la sogs pas// kun kyang rang byung ye shes nyid// stong nyid namakha'i ngang bu cig/ mthun pa dang
6a6(11): mnyen po gnyis// ye nas gnyis med gcig pas na// gdod nas 'jigs pa ga la yod// sems dpa' chen po rigs 'dzin khyod// 'jig med 'khor ba'i la brgyud pa// ma rig ngo bo de bzhin pas// zhi ba med pa'i skad cig ma// de nyid rig pa pade chen gnas// sa
6a7(11): gyis mi khyab chos dbyings rnams/ de bzhin nyid du gcig bas na/ gang gis ye shes don rtogs pa// kun la dbang sgyur thob pa yin// rdzogs pa chen po lta ba thams cad kyi snying po las// sems kyi sems nyid las rig pa rtsal gyi dbang bskur ba'i lelu ste bcu gcig
6b1(11): pa'o// / de nas 'dus pa'i tshogs rnams sa// kun rig sems kyi rgyal po yis// ye shes spyi blugs bka' stsal pa// thig le cig tu rdzogs pa yis// ye shes chen po'i thun dpe ni// mtha' dang dbus med na mkha' 'dra// mi g.yo snyam
6b2(11): mtsho 'dra/ phar 'joms pas na rdo rje 'dra// de don dbyung ye shes la// snang srid gsal bsgo lnga'i yul// shes pa gsal ba chos kyi sku// 'dzin pa med pas spun gyis grub// khyu chen na mkhang lding ba'i tshe// 'phub rla 'og tu kun chung byed// rdzogs chen rtos
6b3(11): pas sku gsum rdzogs// 'byung 'jug med par gzhag par bya// ji bzhin nyams kyi gnas lugs ni// rnam par rtog sa le ba/ sa le ba la rtog pa med// de ni rang byung ye shes te a ming du mi thogs nyams myong bzhin// mkhur ba chu brug ji bzhin du// ye shes
6b4(11): rnal mi'i don la phebs// nor bu rin chen yin tan ya// dgos 'dod thams cad shugs kyi 'byung // de bzhin ye shes ngos zin pa// byib rgod mi 'byung ye shes gsal// dpengar na dug la sngags btab bzhin// nad rnams sel zhing sman 'gyur ltar// chags spab
6b5(11): la sogs dug rnams la// de nyid gsal btab lta ba'i stong // de rtags sgra thob smi lam bzang // gzugs rnams mthong zhing skor ba byed// bdud rtsi 'dren zhing chos ston pa// rtog pa bzang na ci skyes kyang // blang dod dga' brod sems mi bya// snang ba mi 'ag/
6b6(11): rang byung nyid/ khyad smo lan tshwa ji bzhin du// sems las ma g.yos dam pa'i rtags// sems dpa' chen po de nyon cig/ gsal mi rtog mi g.yo ba'i// nyid gsum bsres pa'i chos nyid 'di// ye shes rab byung chen po'i don// rgyu dang 'bras bu dbyed med pas//
6b7(11): mirtog ye shes spumadzugrub ste// rtsol grub 'das pa'i byang chub sems// gzung 'dzin 'das pa'i ye shes gsal// gsal tsam nyid na dmigs pa med// de bzhin nyid du kun rig pa// de khya gang gnas sangs rgyas yin// yon tan rin chen sprin
7a1(11): 6/ bkod pa/ dmig pa byab la ci 'ang med// chos sku snying po byang chub la// de'i sems nyams bstan pa ni// dmigs pa'i ngan la sems gtad kyang // shes pa gtad du mi chung bab/ yul ma mi rtags de bang ba nas// zhes
7a2(11): pa rtog pa smras na yang/ dz+wa lan ci ga shin// rjes su mi 'drang ldan gyi sa~M kra// tsam nyid namatshan ma rnams/ sna la chu ba snang lag tsamad// snang bcas don zin cing 'dzin nyams// nyid goms pa lam du na// sems

7a4(11): nyi zla gzas zin ji bzhin du/ phyi nang gsang sa gsum bstan pa/ thabs kyi lam du bstan pa yin/ rtog pa chen po lta ba thams cad kyi snying po las// nam kha'i mtshan nyid la rig pa brtsal gyi dbang bsrung ba'i le'u ste/
7a5(11): bcu gnyis pa'o// / de nas 'dus pa'i tshogs rnams la// kun rig sems kyi rgyal po yis// 'gro drug g.yangs gcad pa'i phyir// rtsa ba sems las 'das yi// ye shes ngos gzung bka' stsal pa// kun gzhi
7a6(11): dge sdig rnam bzhi la// chos sku'i ngos bzung mthun dpa' ni// rtsa chu rta ga nas ngos 'dzin pa// sman pa mkhas pa ji bzhin dang // nor bu mu mang ma dri bzhin no// byang chub sems kyi rig pa'i don// snga ma'i bag chags yid yin te// phyi ma skye banyon/
7a7(11): mongs yin / rtog pa skye ba sgo lnga ste// gsum du ma song gnyun mang gnas// dmigs 'dzin med la rang gis gsal// ye shes zang thal nyid yin te// rang gi ngo bo chos kyi sku// shes pa rtsis med drung por 'jug/ dper na ti bya tshang 'jug bzhin//
7b1(11): rang gi sems kyi chos nyid la// sgom du med pa'i bsgom pa bya// de don rtog na dngas zhing bde// shes pa mi 'gyur 'gros mi 'jug/ chu las mi 'da' nya bzhin du ka/ don las mi 'da' chos rtags// de rtog ldan pa'i rnal 'byor pas// rgyal pos
7b2(11): mnga' byed btsun mo bzhin// lnga phyi gnyis pa skye ba'i tshe// de rjes mi gcod byang chub sems// 'phros na kun mo chor ma thag/ ma bslad rang bzhin dengs pa ltar// rang sems rtsol ba med pa la// mi g.yo mnyam pa'i don la bzhag/ de ltar rtog
7b3(11): pa'i rnal 'byor pas/ shing bal lta bu'i lus 'jam pa// phyi nang 'byung 'jug dbugs rnams snyoms// chos nyid bde chen gsang ba'i nyams// sems dpa' chen po de nyon cig/ nga'i chos nyid 'bras bu 'di// ma bcos mkha' la nyi shar bzhin
7b4(11): mun pa med par gsal ba yi// lhangs kyi rtogs na lta ba'i mchog/ don las ma yengs sgom pa yi// gang yang a bkag spyod pa'i phul// de las mi 'da' dam tshig yin// dbyings nas rig pa rang la shar// snga phyi nus pa ga la yod// nyon mongs
7b5(11): bag chags rtag pa yi// ji bzhin pa la gnyis ga sgrib// rang bzhin dbyer med nyid las ni// gnyis med shes pa gcig du rdzogs// phyi nang gnyis med sa rtogs pa'o// mkha' la blo bur sprin gtibs ltar// mkha' dag nang du sprin bsang bzhin//
7b6(11): mtshon du med pas brgyan dang bral// med pa ma yin chos nyid 'di// bka' dgu sngos pa'i dang ldan gyis// kun gyis rtsa ba 'di spyad pas// 'di don rang rig thos pa'i mchog/ thams cad 'di las byung ba yin// 'di shes kun shes pa yi mchog/ gas//
7b7(11): ba'i na na gas chen 'di// nyid kyi nyid kya mi mthong bar// gzhan gyis mtho rag la 'gyur// ji spang bsam gyis mi khyam yang // chos nyid rtogs papang mes na// sangs rgyas su dang mnyam myong ba'i// rnal 'argya chen po'i bsam pan yin// rdzogs
8a1(11): chen po lta ba thams cad kyi snying po las/ ye shes spyi blugs kyi chos kyi chos nyid la// rig pa rtsal gyis dbang bsrung ba'i le'u ste bcu gsum pa'o// // de nas kun rig rgyal po la// sems dpa' rdo rje don zhus pa// ma bsgoms
8a2(11): ye shes ji ltar lags/ phyi nang chos kun ji ltar rdzogs/ dbang chen 'bras bu ji lta bu// che ba'i yon tan ji ltar 'byung // de skad gsol ba'i tshig gsan nas// 'dus pa'i tshogs la bka' stsal pa// ma sgoms don dang mi 'bral bas// thi le gcig tu
8a3(11): rdzogs pa yi/ kun gzhi ma bcos chos sku las// sna tshogs snang yang 'gyur ba med// lha dang lha min mi rnams kyis// skye bar byed pa snga ma'i yid// dmyal ba yi dgas byol song gis// skye bar byed pa nyon mongs yin// sgo lnga rjes 'brang rnam rtog ste//
8a4(11): thag pa sbrul du blo snang ba// sbrul snang tsam nyid thag pa bzhin// yul du snang ba'i mtshan ma rnams// rang rig ye shes ngos zin yin// thams cad rang byung ba nyid kyi don// mkha' ltar khyab cing nyi ltar gsal// gsal tsam nyid na nub pa med// med pa
8a5(11): ma yin shes shing rig/ rig tsam nyid na rang gis stong // stong pa nyid na mtha' dbus med// ye shes lhun grub chen po la// bying rgod zhe 'dzin skyon bral bas// gsal 'debs stong chen po la// dang du bzhag pa ci yang med// mnyam bzhag med pas rjes thob med/
8a6(11): sangs rgyas med pas sems can med// thams cad yang byung chen po la// gzhan du g.yo ba rdul tsam med// de yang sems dpa' rdo rje khyod// dper na nyi ma'i snying po la// gzhan gyis ma byas rang gsal zhing // thams cad ye shes ngo bor gsal// ma rig mu/
8a7(11): pa 'dod nas sangs// de yang kun 'dus snying po khyod// dper na rgyal po mthong ba'i tshe// mnyam nyid gus pa'i blo skye zhing // chos nyid gsal bas rtog pa med// rig pa rgyun chags nyid du gnas// de yang sems dpa' rdo rje khyod// dper na na mkha'i sprin bzhin du
8b1(11): byu ba yang gzhi la gnod med ltar// rnam rtogs thams cad sems yin te// ye shes nyi du thams cad gsal// de yang sems dpa' rdo rje khyod// dper na rgun zla 'bring po la// spab la med mched ji bzhin du// rnam rtogs mtshan ma thams cad kyang // thams cad
8b2(11): ye shes nyid du gsal// dper na rin chen gser gling du// sa rdo btsal gyis mi rnyed bzhin// thams cad sems su don rtags na// ting 'dzin dag la 'byung 'jug med// 'khor ba mya ngan 'das pa'i chos// thams cad chos nyid gyur pa la// bsgom pa'i tha snyad
8b3(11): bral ba'i don// thams cad ye shes nyid du gsal// thug las 'das pas gsal du med// sku las 'das pas gzung du med// sgra las 'das pas brjod du med// rtog pa med pas lhun gyis grub// de yang rdo rje snying po khyod// rnam rtog mtshan ma skye ba'i tshe
8b4(11): chos sku rtog pa med pa'i ngang // 'byung ba'i yon tan la spyod tshe// longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku'i ngang / 'gro drug gzugasu snang ba'i tshe/ sprul sku thub pa chen po'i ngang // sdug bsngal sna tshogs skyes pa'i tshe// ye shes bde ba chen po'i ngang // phyi nang sgra skad
8b5(11): sna tshogs pa/ gsang sngags gi 'khor lo yin// rkyen gyis chag sdang skyes pa tshe// rang byung ye shes shar ba yin// shA dang ser ba la sogs pa// kun bzang thugs rje'i rol pa yin// ngam grog g.yangs sa tsher dod yang // rnam par dag pa zhing kham
8b6(11): yin// mtshan ma spangs pa'i pha rol na/ sgom pa bya ba log na med/ sdug bsngal spangs pa'i pha rol na// bde ba bya ba logs na med// gti mug spangs pa'i pha rol na/ ye shes chen po logs na med// rang sems spangs pa'i pha rol na// sangs rgyas
8b7(11): bya ba'i logs na med// chos can spangs pa'i pha rol na// chos nyid rnam rtog logs na med/ gnod rkyen spangs pa'i pha rol na/ snying rje bya ba logs na med// 'khor ba spangs pa'i pha rol na// mya ngan 'das pa'i ming yang med// de yang sems dpa

9a3(11): 'debs na/ sku gsum ye shes rang bzhin las// khams gsum 'khor bar mi 'gyur te// gdod nas ma sA dA ye sangs rgyas// brtsal ba med par ye nas 'grub// mi nub pa la don gsal ba'i// de nyid lhun grub don rtogs na// rtag kyang
9a4(11): ye shes chen po rtag/ chad kyang 'khor brtsad nas chad// ldan na sku gsung thugs dang ldan// yin na ye nas sangs rgyas yin// med na khams gsum 'khor ba med// gol na chos kyi U lu gol// ma bsgoms ye shes po'i don// brjod pa med pa'i
9a5(11): shes rab la/ dmigs pa med pa'i ting 'dzin gsal// shes rab drang thang so ma la// 'du shes mi bskul btul zhugs bskyed// ci yang mi bsgom ci yang yin// ye shes zang thal nyid du bzhag/ thams cad ye nas mnyam nyid la// rgyud 'bras bur
9a6(11): dbyer ru med/ tha snyad gang yang mi gnas pas// brtsal du med pas dngos po med// de nyid mi gnas byang chub sems// sems zhes bya ba'i don rtogs na// sems la gtan tshigs bzung du med// ji srid bar du btang yod na// de srid bar du khrul pa yin//
9a7(11): mi shes ma go dra ba ba tsam// de ltar rtogs pa'i rnal 'byor thugs/ 1pa yis rig pa 'di spyod na// rang byung ye shes rtsa ba ni// byang chub sems dpa' nyid yin pas// de nyid rtog par bya ba'i thabs// phyi nang chos ma lus pa// ji snyed rang byung nyid kyi don//
9a8(11): de las gzhan pa'i chos med do// rdzogs pa chen po lta ba thams cad kyi snying po las// ye shes klong du phyin pa las// ma sgom ngon dang mi 'bral ba'i le'u ste bcu bzhi pa'o// / de nas sems dpas rdo rje la/ kun rig rgyal pos
9b1(11): bka' stsal pa/ chos rnams lhun gyis rdzogs pa ni// rnal 'byor chen po skal ldan de// snying rje'i rlan dang ma bral bas// sems bskyed rnams gnyis de la rdzogs// bying rgod rnam gnyis skyon bral bas// zhi gnas bde ba de la rdzogs/ sgyu ma lta bum/
9b2(11): rab shes pas/ dngos med rtogs pa'i lhag mthong rdzogs// ser sna 'dzin pa'i sems med pas// sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin pa rdzogs// mi dge nyes byas mi 'byung bas// tshul khrims pha rol phyin pa rdzogs// chos kyi dbyings la kun shod pas// bzod pa'i
9b3(11): pha rol phyin pa rdzogs// lta ba'i don lam g.yos pas// brtson 'grus pha rol phyin pa rdzogs// sems nyid don la mi gol bas// bsam btan pha rol phyin pa rdzogs// chos rnams lta bas thag chod pas// shes rab pha rol phyin pa rdzogs// snang ba gang yang
9b4(11): mi 'gogs pas/ thabs kyi pha rol phyin pa rdzogs// mi gnas bla med den rtogs pas// smon lam pha rol phyin pa rdzogs// ma rig mun pa kun 'jom pas// stobs kyi pha rol phyin pa rdzogs// 'khor 'das ye shes lhun rdzogs pas// ye shes pa
9b5(11): rol phyin pa rdzogs// lus ngag de las ma nyams pas// tshogs chen ma lus thams cad rdzogs// de yang sems dpa' rdo rje khyod// dper na yid bzhin nor bu la// dgos 'dod thams cad rdzogs pa bzhin// chos nyid rig pa dbang thob pas// phyi nang dbang rnams
9b6(11): de la rdzogs// mi rtogs ye shes bgegs gsal bas// phyi nang mtsham bcad de la rdzogs// ma rigs rnams rtogs sgrib med pas// don gyi bshags pa de la rdzogs// gnyis med don la blo gnas pas// byin chen dbab pa de la rdzogs// nyon mongs bdud rtsi chen po lnga/
9b7(11): ye shes byin rlabs don la rdzogs// 'byung ba lnga yis kun khyab pas// dbang chen rim pa don gyis rdzogs// phyog bcur rang bzhin lhun grub pas// gzhal yas khang chen de la rdzogs/ rig tshor don gyi lha yin pas// ye shes lha rnams de la rdzogs// sangs rgyas
10a1(11): sems can dbyer med pas/ spyan drangs bstim pa de la rdzogs// chos nyid rnol mi 'gyur bas// bstan par bzhugs pa de la rdzogs// thams cad bzang ngan mi dbye bas// zil gyi mnan pa de la rdzogs// thams cad
10a2(11): 'dres pa chen po la// nan tan phyag rgya de la rdzogs// bskul bskyod thams cad ye shes pas// phyag rgya'i mchod pa de la rdzogs// sems dang chos su don sbyor la/ sbyor sgrol mchod pa de la rdzogs// yon tan thams cad lhun grub pas// mthar phyin smon
10a3(11): lam de la rdzogs// sku gsung thugs kyi don rdzogs pas// bzlas brjod 'phro 'bu de la rdzogs tshogs rnams snod bcud ye yin pas// tshogs kyi mchod pa de la rdzogs// bde chen gnyis med do ga la/ lhag ma'i mchod pa de la rdzogs// mi bzung ye shes chen
10a4(11): po la/ gtong ma 'i mchod pa de la rdzogs// thig le cig la/ 'dus pa la// dkyil 'khor bsdu ba de la rdzogs// ye shes lhun grub go/ ldan pas// bka' nan lus srung de la rdzogs/ gnyis med don du sangs rgyas pas// dag rtsa sngo pa de la rdzogs// mtshan
10a5(11): dang dpe byad thams cad kyis// ye shes lhun grus de la rdzogs/ rdzogs chen po lta ba thams cad kyi snying po las// chos/ thams cad lhun gyis rdzogs pa'i le'u ste bco lnga pa'o// / de nas sems dpa' rdo rje la// kun rig sems kyi rgyal ba
10a6(11): yis/ dbang gi che ba bka' stsal pa// sangs rgyas rnams kyi dgongs pa yin// na mkha' rgya mtsho nya cig bzhin// ma spros ma bsdus rab snang bzhin// byang chub sems las ma g.yos pa'i// kun la khyab pa'i rig pa gsal// dbab mu mar me dug snga
10a7(11): bzhin/ dmigs pa drug la sgo la gsal// rnam rtog nyid kyang ye shes gsal// gcal tsam nyid na nub pa med// sa gzhi chu zla gang ga bzhin// sna tshogs nyid na gzung du med// che ba'i ye shes rgyun mi 'chad// med la mi zad 'byung ba'i gter// mtshan ma thil
10b1(11): gyis gnon pa yis// sems kyi dbang chen dang po yis// 'dod khams nyi shu zil gyis gnon// 'gro drug g.yangs gcod pa yi// ye shes chen pos zin pas// gzugs khams bcu 'dun de mi 'khor// ye shes spyi thugs ngan skams pas// gzu/
10b2(11): med khams bzhir de mi skye// ye shes chen po la bzlos pas// sa bcur rims kyi de mi bgrod// dbang gsum gcig tu rtogs pa yis// ma bcos pa yi chos nyid kyis// bcos pa'i mtshan ma zil gyis mnan// dmigs pa med pa'i na mkha' yis// min/
10b3(11): pa'i 'byung ba zil gyis mnan/ skye ba med pa'i ye shes kyis// skye ba'i phung po zil gyis mnan// rig pa chos kyi chos nyid 'di// dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyis// dur khrod chen po'i de'i sems// sems las ma rtogs/ sangs rgyas med//

10b7(11): 'dod pa bzhin du 'byung // ye shes chen po 'di rtogs pas// che ba'i yon tan rgyun mi chad// ci yang kun 'byung rin chen gter// de bzhin nyid du kun rig na// 'khor ba dang ni mya ngan 'das// so sor snang ba ma yin te// ji bzhin pa de rtogs nges na// de la la

12a1(11): po khyud/ skyon dang yon tan rnams gnyis kyis// chos nyid 'khrul pa'i gzhi gzhag nas// gnyis ka lcang yang mi 'gal phyir// kun kyang yin la thams cad men// dper na nyi ma'i snying pa la// mun snang gnyis ka mi 'gal
12a2(11): bzhin/ gzhi cig gang yang mi 'gags pas// de nyid dus na dngos gzungs med// de yang rdo rje snying po khyod// chu bran rgya mtshor ro cag bzhin// snang srid ye shes chen po la/ byis pa rnams kyis tha dad bzung // de phyir blo yi snang ba yin// 'byung ba nam

12a5(11): ste/ gnyis med snang ba stong khas mi len// thams cad blo yi snang ba ste// de bas rang sems rtogs pa'i thabs// kun gzhi chos sku ngos zin pa'i// thaMd rang 'byung dbyer med mdzod// de yu 'jug cing rtog 'dod pas// sgo gsum sde mag
12a6(11): phye nas kyang / ye shes lhun grub rdzong chen du// rang gi rgyal po shes/ 'phyo// de yang 'dus pa'i tshogs rnams nyon// ma rtog par ni dag pa'i phyir/ mdo sde dang ni rgyud sde las/ mtshan ma bzhi'i gtan tshigs kyis// che
12a7(11): pa gong 'og khyad par gyis/ ming da tha snyad bsam yas kyang // zhen pa bzlog pa'i thabs su zad// rdo rje theg pa'i las med de/ de bzhin rtog pa'i rnal 'byor pa/ yal bar 'dug pa lam yang men// de don rgyun du ma ya na// dgongs

12b2(11): nyid 'bras bu ye rdzogs pa/ dog gnyis bral de kho na// dor bar bya ba'i dngos med par// blang bar bya ba ga la yod// sems dpa' rdo rje nga la ni// lam med lam ltar ma sbyar cig/ sa med sa bcur ma bgrod cig/ rten 'brel dmigs

13b4(11): zla'o// gtsang dang mi gtsang gnyis bzhi// lung pa la sogs gang rung la// gya khyi rnams kyi zasu mtho // de phyir blang myed pa yin// mtshan dang dpe byad yon tan dang // lus dang bag chags skyon rnams kun// dang 'jog med papa la zla'o// bzhi ma 'khrul pas ma rig

3a3(12): stegs gnyis spyod pa'i 'dren sgong snang ba ni// sprul sku'i dam chos nyan rab sems// thabs kyi sbyor sgor snang ba ni// kri ya u la yo ga nyid// nges pa'i gsang sgor snang ba ni// bskyed dang rdzogs dang rdzogs pa'i tshe// sgo ba
3a4(12): dag nas zhugs pa yis// mnyam pa'i spyi mdzod chen por 'gro// gzung ba yul gyi khang pa'i nad// 'dzin pa sems kyis gzer sgro yis// thaMd kun la khyab mos kyang // tha ram+ba sgo lcags/ phyed par bka'// mtha'i mun pu s+thi
3a5(12): 'dum gyis/ ma slabs shes pa'i rtsal 'chang ba// lha'i bi shas kar ma ltar// bde shegs byang chub sems dpa' dang / sprul pa rigs 'dzin ma lus pa'i// dgong brdal ngag gi lde mig khyer// bla ma mnyes par byas gyur na
3a6(12): lde mig rtsil ba'i dus la ba2// mdzod 'dri mthong bar bya ba yang // dbus kyi lte ba mdzod chen la/ mu khyud brdal dgra nges pa gsum// gling ga zhi srid pa rab byung nyid// khang khyim bco brgyad thugs rjes bskor// kha
3a7(12): khyim bzhi'i rtsa ba can// grong khyer bzha'i mu khrung mdzes// ma hA yo ga'i po spang dang / a nu yo ga'i ji smad dang // a ti yo ga ling smad dang / gsang sko dpe don rtags gsum gyis// ngos spyod thob pa'i

3b2(12): pa dgongs pa ma nor ba// byib rgod med pa'i dpal gzhags// 'bras bu thog ma'i rangs nyid// 'khrul/ gzhi'i thog tu sangs// lha la dpag bsam shing bu dang // gnod sbyin bum pa bzang po dang // klu
3b3(12): la yid bzhin nor bu dang // snod 'dzim grub pa lag pa bzhin// rnam rtog bag chags sbubs 'di na// ma rig sgol sbubs phye bas// rig pa'i ye shes rnyed par 'gyur// rang bzhin par dor bden
3b4(12): pa mthong / ting 'dzin par dor brtan pa thob// chos nyid bar dod dran pa sad// srid pa'i bar dor ye shes sbubs// srid pa'i dra ba 'joms pa'o// sprul pas yid la bsam pa rdzogs// 'gro don maka?
3b5(12): rdzogs pa ni// sngar 'dris mi dpa' phrad bzhin gyur// ma ni kun khyab chen mo ste// bu ni rig pa cir bu nyid// sngon gyi bag chags goms dbang gi/ dud 'gro'i bu ltar nu ma 'tshol// yang na rang bzhin srog thon
3b6(12): byed/ ma'i spang du pu 'grod// ma bu brdal 'jal man ngag 'dis// rin chen gsahA sbubs nang du// 'dod pa thams cad rab tu 'grub// thog ma'i 'bas sleb ces bya// sngon las 'phral rkyen brtson 'grus
3b7(12): kyis// skal ldan rig kyi khu mchog yin// 'jig rten bya ba btang byas la// thos/ sam sgom pa sna tshogs kyis// ji legs bskor slab par ces// phyi rab kun la gdams par bzhag/ zhes sems
4a1(12): phyogs chen po mdzod kyi rgyud// ye shes na mkha' las// mdzod rtsa ba'i le'u ste dang po'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis 'ardul nges pa'i ti

9a4(12): po gti mug che// gti mug blo de gti mug sel// byol song gnas las nges par grol// gsal bas zhe sdang lam du sh+ya// mchod pa chen po zhe sdang che// nyon mongs kun gyi sgra che ba// dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal

9a6(12): yin/ mchod pa chen po chags pa che// chags pa thams cad sel bar byed// ser sna yi dgas gnas sgrol// mchod pa chen po 'de la che// dga' 'a chen mo dgu 'che// khong khro lha min yul lus grol// thog med
9a7(12): phra rog lam du bya// mchod pa chen po khro ba che/ khro ba chen po dgra che ba// phra dog lha'i gnas las grol// rig sngags bde gshegs skur snang ba// stong pa rdo rje sems dpa'i sku// gsal ba rnam par snang
9b1(12): nyid/ bde ba snang za' yas la// mi 'gag pa ni rin chen 'byung // thog med don yod grub pa nyid// rigs lnga'i sangs rgyas 'di dag rnams// sems nyid dang du snang ba yin// yum chen ltar ni snang ba ya
9b2(12): sbyang pa na mkha'i dbyings phyug ma// gsal gas ni sangs rgyas spyan// bde ba me ni gos dkar mo// mi 'gag chu ni ma ma ki/ thogs med rlung gi dam tshig sgrol// sems dpa' sems ma'i tshogs chen
9b3(12): ni/ sras kyi tshogs su snang ba yang // stong pa khro la sgo bar snang // gsal gsa'i snying po la// bde ba spyan ras gzigs nyid// ma 'gag na mkha'i snying po dang // thogs med phyag rdo rje'o// stong pa
9b4(12): gshin rje khros pa nyid// gsal ba lha mo sgeg mo la// bde ba pe wang klu len ma// ma 'gag mi phreng ba ma// thogs pa med pa gar mkhan nyid// stong pa khro bo stobs po che// gsal ba byams pa'i skuru
9b5(12): snang / mi 'gag sgrib pa rnam hA sel// thogs pa med pa 'jam dpal nyid// stong pa khro mo stobs chen ma// gsal ba lha mo spos ma nyid// bde ba lha mo mar me ma// mi 'gag pa ni me tog ma// thogs pa med padr-i
9b6(12): cha ma/ stong pa rta 'asprin chen po la// gsal ba rta 'gyen yum yin te// bde ba bdud rtsi 'khyil ba la// mi 'gag pa ni yum du gnas// thogs pa med pa sgo ba'i las// stong pa lha dang lha min thub// gsal
9b7(12): ba ma'i thub pa ste// bde ba yi dgas thub pa la// mi 'gag pa ni byol song thub/ thog med dmyal ba'i thub pa'o// stong pa kun tu bzang po la// gsal ba kun tu bzang mo ste// bde ba yab yum 'du 'bra
10a1(12): med/ mi 'gag dkyil 'khor lha tshogs rnams// thogs pa med par 'byin pa'o// stong pa rnam shes phung po la// gsal ba gzugs kyis phung po nyid// bde ba 'du
10a2(12): shes phung po la// ma 'gag la ni tshong ba ste// thogs pa med pa 'du byed do// stong pa lus kyi dbang po la// gsal ba mig gi dbang po nyid/ bde ba lha'i dbang po nyid// mi 'gag pa ni snang yin
10a3(12): la/ thogs pa med pa rna ba'o// stong pa nyid la gsal ba 'tsheng // bde ba mchin pa mi 'gag mkhal// thog pa med pa glo ba'o// stong d+ha rang byung ye shes rtsa// gsal ba rtsa bzhi 'dus pa'i mdo// bde
10a4(12): ba rang rgyud las kyi rtsa// ma 'gag rang byung chos nyid rtsa// thog pa med pa yon tan rtsa// stong pa na mkha'i dngas lags 'byed// gsal ba'i dngas ma'i rtse// bde ba ma'i dngas ma la// mi 'gag chu'i dngas
10a5(12): ma de/ thogs med rlung gi dngas mAr shar // stong pa srog 'dzan rlung yin la// gsal ba sa dang 'dres pa'i rlung // bde ba me dang drod mnyam la// mi 'gag chu dpa 'grog pa'i rlung // thogs med rlung gi rlung
10a6(12): du bshadastong pa lus lan mkha' rlung // gsal ba sna la sa'i rlung / bde ba mige la me'i rlung // mi 'gag lce la chu'i rlung // thog med snang bar rlung gi rlung // stong pa na mkha'i rtsa gsum nyid// nyi ma zla
10a7(12): bar yul// gsal ba sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor la// bde ba 'gyen par longs spyod pas// mi 'gag snying khar chos 'khor nyid// thogs pa med pa bde chen spyi// gnas pa rtsa'i dkyil 'khod kyis// lus kun
10b1(12): la na khyab par gnas// spyod pa byang chub sems yin la// gsal ba dri chen bdud rtsir gnas// bde ba pad+ma rak+ta nyid// mi 'gag she chen dam rdzas la// thogs med dri chur gnas pa rnams// sangs rgyas ragras
10b2(12): lnga'i dam rdzas de// khams kyi bdud rtsi chen po nyid// rnal 'byor 'dus pa kun rdzab gnas// stong pa mi'i sha ru bshad// gsal ba glang po'i sha yin la// bde ba ba glang sha yin te// mi 'gag pa ni rta'i sha/
10b3(12): thoglo med bya 'am khyi shar bshad// khams dgu 'dus pa dngas ma ni// rnal 'byor pa yis nyam su blangs// bdud rtsi'i gtor ma'i mchod pa ni// rig 'dzin bka' srungs zhi khro mchod// de nas gdams ngag gdab par
10b4(12): bya stong pa hUM gi rang bzhin la// gsal ba yi ge oM yan te// bde la a'i rnam pa la// ma 'gag pa ni swa yu gnas// thogs pa med ya ge hA// stong pa lha dang lha ma yin// a dkar su ser gnas pa yin//
10b5(12): gsal ba byol song dud kha'i du// bde ba ya dgas tra dmar la// mi 'gag mi'i mr-i ldeng de// thogs med dmyal ba'i dri nag po// stong pas nyamA na sems la 'char// gsal bas gar ni lus la 'char// bde
10b6(12): bas sngags ni ngag las 'char// mi 'gag mthong snang yul la 'chang // thogs med bag chags rmi lam 'char// rnal 'byor nyams ni snang ba yin// thams cad ma lus 'khor 'das kyis// nyams snang 'di
10b7(12): ma pa ma gang / sta mas thugs kyi ni shes dag rnams kyi mni shes la 'ayid// gsalabs lus kyi rdzu 'phrul lam 'di sa sun gyis ni shes ma// mi 'phag sanas kyi ma shes so/
11a1(12): med snyan gyi mngon shes dang // mngon par shes pa rnam drug/ gdul bya yul du gzigs pa yin// stong pas chos kyi sku yin te// gsal bas longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku// bde/
11a2(12): bas long sku yul dang ldan// mi 'gag sprul pa'i sku ru snang // thogs pa med pas 'gro don mdzad// stong pas chos dbyings ye shes la// gsal me long lta gu ste// bde bas so sor rtog pa la// mi 'gag
11a3(12): pas na mnyam pa nyid// thogs med khyab grub pa'o// stong pas stag pa'i mtha' dang bral// gsal bas chad pa'i mtha' dang bral// bde bas stag chad gnyis su med// mi 'gag med pa'i mtha' dang bral// thogs me
11a4(12): yod pa'i mtha' dang bral// stong pa yul nyid snang stong dang // gsal ba sems nyid gsal stong dang // bde bas lus nyid bde stong dang // mi 'gag stong par mi gnas te// thogs med snang ba thar zug med// stong pa yul las grol
11a5(12): pa dang / gsal ba sems las grol ba dang // bde ba lus las grol ba ste// mi 'gag stong la sbyad pa yin// thogs med snang ba a mthas min// stong pa phur rna nye bar zhi// gsal ba rdo rje khro gdeng ma// bde b.ro zan shan ting

11a7(12): tshang ma dud 'grin ma/ mi 'gyur gser gyi gdam 'angs yin// ma 'gag par ni 'char ba yang / skar mda' lta bu'i gdam ngag yin// thogs pa med par 'byung ba ni// gangs la nyi ma shar ba yin// stong pa ngo spod yul bzhir
11b1(12): bden ma hA yo ga'i pa sprod nga / a mu yo ga'i nga sprod dang / a ti yo ga'i po spod dang / sku gsum dbyer med do sprod bzhin/ bden pa ni tshul gyi rnam pa can// gsal ba jos dra brda' ste// longs sku 'dra 'bag
11b2(12): byed srur spang // sprul sku 'od khyim kha myang spang / chos spu rin chen men shel spang // 'du 'bral med pa nyi ma yi// snying po nyid la sprad par bya// brda' dang ngag bla stan pa ni// shes pa brgyad pa rtogs pa 'chag
11b3(12): bde ba spang ba'i dgo ba ni// sku gsum 'du 'bral med pa yis// bag chags sbubs kyi dgongs pa mchod// longs sus lnga ldan dgongs pa chod// sprul srus rdzogs ldan dgongs pachod// chos sus rdzogs ldan chen po
11b4(12): chod/ bde ldan rnam pa bcu gnyis ldan// mi 'gag pa la spang pa'i skyon// sngar 'dris mi bzhin mi rtogs pas// skyon bzhi dag dang ldan pas na ka de nyid rnam pa bcu drug rig/ thogs pa med pas mtha' ba zhi bral//

12a2(12): 'jug/ mi 'gag la ni 'bras bu nyid// thogs med tshe cig sangs rgyas thob// zhes sems phyogs chen po mdzod kyi rgyud las// ye shes na mkha'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// // de nas 'khor tshogs dpag med pas// ston pa la ni rab tu

1b3(13): 'jig pa// gsang ba'i bslab pa yin// rtog pa la sog su 'dod pa// de la de gsog nam yang med// skyes na 'gag cing 'gag na skye// de ni bdag bcas 'khrul pa'i blo bdag med gang skye skye rgyu cing // mi

2a1(13): / 'khor bkye 'gag rgya mi shig/ de bas rtogs pas 'bor bar 'dzings// shes rtogs lta bu'i sdig pani// stong gsum ma lus srog gcad pas// sdig pas de brdus cha mi phod// lba bsgob 'bras bu de dang mtshungs//
2a2(13): rdzos bya rtog byed gnyis med cing / rtogs lha la sogs mi skyen// dgos ched byed du de bsogs gsungs/ ma rtogs ma bsgoms ma shes na// rdo rje kun du bzang po yin// bdag med dmigs dang rnam shes ji ltar skyed// dra bya
2a3(13): dran byed med de shes dang mi shes bral// rtogs bya rtogs byed med de dgos ched de rtogs brjod// rtogs pa ma skyes pa ni rtogs pa'i mchog/ 'ching grol med pa grol ba'i dam pa yin// bcings na grol zhing grol na 'ching // yul sems
2a4(13): gnyis su med pa ni// byang chub sems zhes bde gshegs gsungs// yul sems gnyis su 'dod pa dang / yul med sems la gsal stong dang // yod med rtag chad 'khrul pa'i sems// 'khrul dang ma 'khrul gnyis med la/
2a5(13): ma 'khrul dgos ched gnyis yod 'khrul// de de nyid de dgos ched kyis// de mtshon 'khrul pa blo bung dang // med pa dang na cing mi rung // skabs kyi re shig brjod par zad // yul sems gnyisu med pa na// de men chos med gnyisu med// snod bcu

2a7(13): lhun grub rdzogs pa chen// rtog sgom 'bras bu 'dod pa dang // thar par 'dod pa'i yid can la// byang chub nam ya ma yin// rdo rje sems dpa'i gsang ba'i thigs pa 'di// dga' rab rdo rje'i thugs la dbyer med thim// zhes lta ba lhag pa byang
2b1(13): chub sems kyi gsang ba'i thogs pa zhes bya ba ste/ le'u dang ba na/ bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje sems dpa' sa byag 'tshal lo// 'khor 'das rnas pa gnyis pa yang // chos can rtogs
2b2(13): tsha nyidi rtogs// bya ba mdo dang lhun gyis grub// dor rtogs rtag rtogs 'dus ma byas// byang chub sems dang 'phrul pa'i sems/ rang byu rten byung la sogs kyis// 'khor 'das gnyis su shes med shes// sman brdo tsam na dug brdo snga

2b6(13): 'dzin// de bas rang nyid gnyis med na// shes bya shes byed la sogs med// sbyangs nas rtogs thob phyis 'dod dang // rtogs thob thabs la rten pa dang / bya ba ma bral thabs kyis kyang // yang dag 'bras bu thob med// bya med byed bral
2b7(13): 'bras bu de// chos nyid don rtogs bde chen 'grub// 'dod pa ma zad 'bras bu dang // 'dod pas grub pa'i 'bras bu dang / 'dod pa med pas len pa ni / bya bral lhan grub shes par gyis// mdor na chos rnaMs thaMd ni// 'khor dang mya ngan 'das

1b3(14): kyi nam mkha' chen po chos kyi pho brang // bai dUr+ya zhun ma dang phyogs 'thun pa// tsan+da dkar po'i dri dang // gu gul dkar po'i dri dang // dkar gsum reng bu'i dri dang / dri zhim po de rnams
1b4(14): dang phyogs mthun pa'i dri zhim sna tshogs kyi rgyan pa/ gser la ga yu yis spras pa dang / phyogs 'thun pa'i chos nyid dag pa'i gzhal yas khang chen po de na// dpal kun tu bzang
2a1(14): the chos nyid mnyam pa'i ngang la bzhugs pa la/ dpal rdo rje sems dpa' zhes bya ba des// mos pa chen po sngon du btang nas/ sems can gyi nyon mongs pa gzhom pa'i phyir bskor ba
